<p>The <b>2002–03 UEFA Champions League</b> was the 11th season of <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>'s premier European club <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> tournament, the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, since its rebranding in 1992, and the 48th European Cup tournament overall. The competition was won by <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>, who beat <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(football)" title="Penalty shootout (football)">penalties</a> in the European Cup's first ever all-Italian final, to win their sixth European title, and its first in nine years. Manchester United's <a href="/wiki/Ruud_van_Nistelrooy" title="Ruud van Nistelrooy">Ruud van Nistelrooy</a> was again the top scorer, scoring 12 goals over the two group stages and knockout stage, in addition to two goals he had scored in the qualifying phase, although his side bowed out in the quarter-finals and missed out on the chance of playing in a final at their own stadium.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> were the defending champions, but were eliminated by Juventus in the semi-finals.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Association_team_allocation">Association team allocation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Association team allocation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A total of 72 teams participated in the 2002–03 Champions League, from 51 <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> associations (Liechtenstein organizes no domestic league competition). Countries are allocated places according to their 2002 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_coefficient#League_coefficient" title="UEFA coefficient">UEFA league coefficient</a>, which takes into account their performance in European competitions from 1996–97 to 2000–01.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>Below is the qualification scheme for the 2002–03 UEFA Champions League:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Access_list_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Access_list-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li>Associations 1–3 each have four teams qualify</li>
<li>Associations 4–6 each have three teams qualify</li>
<li>Associations 7–15 each have two teams qualify</li>
<li>Associations 16–48 each have one team qualify (except Liechtenstein, San Marino and Andorra)</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Round_and_draw_dates">Round and draw dates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Round and draw dates">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

</div>
</div>
<p>16 winners from the third qualifying round, 10 champions from countries <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_coefficients" title="UEFA coefficients">ranked</a> 1–10, and six second-placed teams from countries ranked 1–6 were drawn into eight groups of four teams each. The top two teams in each group advance to the Champions League second group stage, while the third-placed teams advance to round three of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_Cup" title="UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a>.</p>
<p>Tiebreakers, if necessary, are applied in the following order:</p>
<ol>
<li>Points earned in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Total goals scored in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Away goals scored in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Cumulative goal difference in all group matches.</li>
<li>Total goals scored in all group matches.</li>
<li>Higher <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_coefficients" title="UEFA coefficients">UEFA coefficient</a> going into the competition.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a>, <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Haifa_F.C." title="Maccabi Haifa F.C.">Maccabi Haifa</a> made their debut in the group stage. Maccabi Haifa became the first Israeli club to qualify for the group stage.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

</tr>
<tr bgcolor="#CCCCFF">
<td>Third-placed teams enter the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Cup" title="2002–03 UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Cup#Third_round" title="2002–03 UEFA Cup">third round</a></td>
</tr>
</table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_group_stage">Second group stage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Second group stage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League_second_group_stage" title="2002–03 UEFA Champions League second group stage">2002–03 UEFA Champions League second group stage</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_(Juventus_F.C.,_no._26)_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_(A.C._Milan)_-_20030528.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2464" data-file-width="1648" height="254" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/170px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/255px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/340px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_(Juventus_F.C.,_no._26)_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_(A.C._Milan)_-_20030528.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Edgar Davids (№ 26) clashing with Gennaro Gattuso in the <a href="/wiki/2003_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2003 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The eight group winners and eight group runners-up were drawn into four groups, with each one containing two group winners and two group runners-up. The top two teams in each group advanced to the Champions League knockout stage.</p>
<p>Tiebreakers, if necessary, are applied in the following order:</p>
<ol>
<li>Points earned in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Total goals scored in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Away goals scored in head-to-head matches between the tied teams.</li>
<li>Cumulative goal difference in all group matches.</li>
<li>Total goals scored in all group matches.</li>
<li>Higher <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_coefficients" title="UEFA coefficients">UEFA coefficient</a> going into the competition.</li>
</ol>
<table class="wikitable">
<tr>
<th>Key to colours in group tables</th>
</tr>
<tr bgcolor="#CCFFCC">
<td>Group winners and runners-up advance to the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League#Knockout_stage" title="2002–03 UEFA Champions League">knockout stage</a></td>
</tr>
</table>
